\DoxyCodeLine{02767\ \ \ \ \ values\_.close\_to\_negative\_zero\ =}

\DoxyCodeLine{02769\ \ \ \ \ values\_.further\_from\_negative\_zero\ =}

\DoxyCodeLine{02771\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{02791\ }
\DoxyCodeLine{02792\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Makes\ some\ NAN's.\ \ Sets\ the\ most\ significant\ bit\ of\ the\ fraction\ so\ that}}
